1.5-1.5 1.9.7-.1 1.4-.3 2-.5-.4.4-1 1-1.7 1.5z"></path>\n</svg>\n</span>\n</a>\n</li>\n<li class="social__item social__item--email " data-link-name="email">\n<a class="social__action data-link-name="messenger">\n<a class="social__action js-social__action--top social-icon-wrapper" data-link-name="social top" class="meta-button social-tray__button">\n<span class="u-h">Close</span>\n<span class="inline-close inline-icon inline-close--small centered-icon social-tray__icon">\n<svg class="inline-close--small__svg centered-icon__svg social-tray__icon__svg inline-close__svg inline-icon__svg" height="18" viewBox="0 0 18 18" width="18">\n<path d="M7.5 9L1 2l1-1 7 6.5L16 1l1 1-6.5 7 meta__number" data-commentcount-format="content" data-discussion-closed="false" data-discussion-id="/p/69dn3">\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p class="byline" data-component="meta-byline" data-link-name="byline">Anonymous Academic</p>\n<p aria-hidden="true" class="content__dateline">\n<time class="content__dateline-wpd js-wpd" data-timestamp="1492149625000" datetime="2017-04-14T07:00:25+0100" itemprop="datePublished">\nFriday 14 April 2017 <span class="content__dateline-time">07.00\xa0BST</span>\n</time>\n<time class="content__dateline-lm js-lm u-h" data-timestamp="1492507523000" datetime="2017-04-18T10:25:23+0100" itemprop="dateModified">\nLast modified on Tuesday 18 April 2017 <span class="content__dateline-time">10.25\xa0BST</span>\n</time>\n</p>\n<meta content="2017-04-18T10:25:23+0100" itemprop="dateModified"/>\n</div>\n<div class="content__article-body from-content-api js-article__body" data-test-id="article-review-body" itemprop="articleBody">\n<p><span class="drop-cap"><span class="drop-cap__inner">\u201cM</span></span>ake sure you actually go this time,\u201d called my head of department as I left the office. \u201cI will,\u201d I yelled back. \u201cI\u2019m actually going to do it.\u201d I was about to go to my first international conference in a decade.</p>\n<p>As anyone who travels for work knows, having children adds a layer of complexity to even one night spent away from home. But as a single parent living thousands of miles away from my family, the logistics around professional travel can be especially difficult.<br/></p>\n<aside class="element element-rich-link element--thumbnail element-rich-link--not-upgraded" data-component="rich-link" data-link-name="rich-link-2 | 1">\n<div class="rich-link">\n<div class="rich-link__container">\n<div class="rich-link__header">\n<h1 class="rich-link__title">I'm a single parent and a scientist and I'm dangerously stressed</h1>\n</div>\n<div class="rich-link__read-more">\n<div class="rich-link__arrow">\n<span class="inline-arrow-in-circle inline-icon ">\n<svg class="inline-arrow-in-circle__svg inline-icon__svg" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24">\n<path class="rich-link__arrow-icon" d="M12 0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12s5.373 12 12 12 12-5.373 12-12S18.627 0 12 0m.21 19l-.637-.668 4.888-6.326H4.996v-1.01h11.465l-4.888-6.333.637-.668L19 11.153v.685l-6.79 7.157" fill="#005689" fill-rule="evenodd"></path>\n</svg> </span>\n</div>\n<div class="rich-link__read-more-text">\nRead more\n</div>\n</div>\n<a class="rich-link__link u-faux-block-link__overlay" href="https://www.theguardian.com/higher-education-network/2017/jan/13/im-a-single-parent-and-a-scientist-and-im-dangerously-stressed"></a>\n</div>\n</div>\n</aside>\n<p> I\u2019d made plans to travel for work in the past, but they\u2019d always fallen through last minute. Sometimes my babysitter had been unwell, sometimes I\u2019d been let down by my son\u2019s father, and sometimes I just didn\u2019t feel I could leave my child for an extended period.</p>\n<p>Conferences are <a class="u-underline" data-link-name="in body link" href="https://www.theguardian.com/higher-education-network/blog/2011/aug/26/speaking-at-academic-conferences">an important part of our lives as scholars</a>. They are where we connect with those whose research area is closest to our own, where we receive feedback on work in progress, and where we learn about the latest developments in our fields. Conferences can be intellectual lifelines where we make ourselves and our work visible to potential collaborators and future colleagues.</p>\n<p>In Australia, where I live, there is little support to assist with overnight childcare. The situation is similar at most institutions in the UK and the US. A handful of places have support schemes, but even the most generous have limitations and rarely cover the costs involved.</p>\n<p>But after a couple of short, successful domestic trips, I felt ready to try going further afield to a conference in the American mid-west. I worked out the minimum amount of time it would take to get there, deal with jet-lag, give my paper, then travel home. I talked the plans through with my son, cleared it with my regular, trusted babysitter, and booked my tickets.</p>\n<p>I could, of course, have taken my son with me. But it was term time, and it didn\u2019t seem right to take him out of school. I also remembered an awkward incident at one of my lectures when he was four years old. After diligently colouring in for about 40 minutes, he asked in his loudest, clearest voice: \u201cHave you nearly finished, Mummy? Because this is boring.\u201d He\u2019s older now, but I still didn\u2019t think I could expect him to sit quietly at the back of a seminar room for three days. </p>\n<p> During an airport stopover towards the end of my journey, I got a text from the babysitter to say my son has become unwell. I wanted to turn around and go back home. I talked to the babysitter, who told me not to return and that my son would be fine. My son agreed and told me to keep going. So I did.</p>\n<aside class="element element-pullquote element--supporting">\n<span class="inline-quote inline-icon inline-tone-fill">\n<svg class="inline-tone-fill__svg inline-quote__svg inline-icon__svg" height="10" viewBox="0 0 33 20" width="17">\n<path d="M9.002 20c3.85.068 6.932-3.104 7-6.994.068-3.892-3.15-6.937-7-7.006-2.016-.036-3.59.694-4.888 2.053A9.968 9.968 0 0 1 4.001 6.5C4.064 2.97 7.414.937 11.003 1l-1-1C3.98 0 .098 4.447.002 10.006c-.097 5.557 3.35 9.892 9 9.994zm17 0c3.85.068 6.932-3.104 7-6.994.068-3.892-3.15-6.937-7-7.006-2.016-.036-3.59.694-4.888 2.053a9.968 9.968 0 0 1-.113-1.553c.063-3.53 3.413-5.563 7.002-5.5l-1-1c-6.022 0-9.904 4.447-10 10.006-.097 5.557 3.35 9.892 9 9.994z"></path>\n</svg> </span>\n<blockquote>\n<p class="pullquote-paragraph">I am not as visible a scholar as I should be and I\u2019ve had few opportunities to share my work ahead of publication</p>\n</blockquote>\n<span class="inline-quote inline-icon closing inline-tone-fill">\n<svg class="closing__svg inline-tone-fill__svg inline-quote__svg inline-icon__svg" height="10" viewBox="0 0 33 20" width="17">\n<path d="M9.002 20c3.85.068 6.932-3.104 7-6.994.068-3.892-3.15-6.937-7-7.006-2.016-.036-3.59.694-4.888 2.053A9.968 9.968 0 0 1 4.001 6.5C4.064 2.97 7.414.937 11.003 1l-1-1C3.98 0 .098 4.447.002 10.006c-.097 5.557 3.35 9.892 9 9.994zm17 0c3.85.068 6.932-3.104 7-6.994.068-3.892-3.15-6.937-7-7.006-2.016-.036-3.59.694-4.888 2.053a9.968 9.968 0 0 1-.113-1.553c.063-3.53 3.413-5.563 7.002-5.5l-1-1c-6.022 0-9.904 4.447-10 10.006-.097 5.557 3.35 9.892 9 9.994z"></path>\n</svg> </span>\n</aside>\n<p>I boarded the plane for the final part of the journey and worried all the way to my destination. My son spent the next day home from school and \u2013 as the sitter predicted \u2013 soon recovered. At the conference, I gave my paper and began to relax. I talked to colleagues and re-connected with my academic peer group.</p>\n<p>I\u2019m dwelling on this incident quite a bit at the moment, partly because I\u2019m drafting an application for a promotion. The documentation at my institution is extensive, and while academics must argue their case for advancement the process is supposed to be affirming. But as I write I reflect on all the things I haven\u2019t done and all the trips I couldn\u2019t take. </p>\n<p>I am not as visible a scholar as I should be and I\u2019ve had few opportunities to share my work ahead of publication over the past few years. I\u2019ve tried to be smart about this \u2013 tailoring my research to a more local literature, taking advantage of nearby archives \u2013 but there are times when I crave the company and feedback of my immediate peers, and that can only be achieved through travel.</p>\n<p>I am fortunate to have a generous fellowship, which came with a large travel stipend. Yet almost all of it will be returned to the funding body when my fellowship comes to an end later this year. </p>\n<p>My brief trip to the US left me with a hefty babysitting bill. Such payments are not tax deductible, even though conference travel is regarded as an essential part of career development in many professions. Some institutions offer limited support to enable lone parents to travel, although <a class="u-underline" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.sciencemag.org/careers/2014/08/new-initiatives-offer-child-care-solutions-traveling-scientists">the sciences seem to have been at the forefront</a>. For humanities, <a class="u-underline" data-link-name="in body link" href="https://women.acm.org/ACMW-Webpage/Newsletters/Articles/2014-01-Family-Friendly-Conference-ACMWConnections.pdf">there are a few scholarly conferences that make efforts to be family friendly</a> (pdf), offering childcare or providing spaces for children to play, for example. </p>\n<aside class="element element-rich-link element--thumbnail element-rich-link--not-upgraded" data-component="rich-link" data-link-name="rich-link-2 | 2">\n<div class="rich-link">\n<div class="rich-link__container">\n<div class="rich-link__header">\n<h1 class="rich-link__title">I lost my job in academia after having a baby \u2013 now I'm stuck</h1>\n</div>\n<div class="rich-link__read-more">\n<div class="rich-link__arrow">\n<span class="inline-arrow-in-circle inline-icon ">\n<svg class="inline-arrow-in-circle__svg inline-icon__svg" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24">\n<path class="rich-link__arrow-icon" d="M12 0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12s5.373 12 12 12 12-5.373 12-12S18.627 0 12 0m.21 19l-.637-.668 4.888-6.326H4.996v-1.01h11.465l-4.888-6.333.637-.668L19 11.153v.685l-6.79 7.157" fill="#005689" fill-rule="evenodd"></path>\n</svg> </span>\n</div>\n<div class="rich-link__read-more-text">\nRead more\n</div>\n</div>\n<a class="rich-link__link u-faux-block-link__overlay" href="https://www.theguardian.com/higher-education-network/2017/feb/10/i-was-made-redundant-after-having-a-baby-i-worry-i-wont-find-another-job"></a>\n</div>\n</div>\n</aside>\n<p>One of my senior colleagues, who has dealt with the endless juggling act that comes with single-parenthood, told me that nothing will truly change until those who have experienced such difficulties are in positions of power. That\u2019s a slightly depressing thought, given that the amount of time absorbed by raising a child <a class="u-underline" data-link-name="in body link" href="https://chroniclevitae.com/news/569-are-children-career-killers">usually prohibits a rapid rise to the upper echelons.</a></p>\n<p>Meanwhile, I\u2019m planning another trip. I have a whole raft of details to work out, but having done it once, I can do it again. And next time it will be easier, surely. </p>\n<p><strong>Join the <a class="u-underline" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://preview.gutools.co.uk/higher-education-network#https://register.theguardian.com/higher-education/?CMP=dis_57">higher education network</a> for more comment, analysis and job opportunities, direct to your inbox. class="u-underline" data-link-name="in body link" href="mailto:highereducationnetwork@theguardian.com">highereducationnetwork@theguardian.com</a></strong></p>\n</div>\n<div class="submeta">\n<span
